# openAI * Prompt 1
 * Page Link: https://sora.com/g/gen_01jqyt16erevbbr08jbs48t4qr
 * Prompt:A raw amateur phone photo shot on iPhone with no filters, far shot of a 19-year-old Eastern European girl standing alone. The girl is pale with delicate features, wearing no visible makeup. Her vibe is introspective and distant, like she’s halfway between here and somewhere else. She has long, wispy ash-brown hair with choppy bangs that fall into her eyes, which barely meet the camera. Her posture is slouched, one hand hanging limp by her side, the other holding a cigarette she isn’t smoking. She’s wearing a faded gray oversized sweater with loose threads and a long pleated black skirt with scuffed combat boots. She’s standing at the edge of a nondescript rooftop in Bucharest, concrete walls around her, tagged with graffiti. The camera is behind her, catching her in profile as she half-turns. The sky is washed out white, noon sun trying to punch through thin cloud cover, casting cold, inconsistent shadows. The mood is bleak, but quietly intimate. No filters. Very raw photo shot on iPhone 16. The photo looks accidental, like someone caught her in a moment she didn’t care about. Posted to Snapchat in 2021. Off-balance framing, flat lighting, mediocre image quality. UGC, IMG_3032.png, raw style, super amateur Snapchat 2021, ugc, shot with an iPhone 16, no bokeh.

# openAI * Prompt 2
 * Page Link: https://sora.com/g/gen_01jr2cm2nyfxdvsmb1mjswk0pz
 * Prompt:Design a visually appealing and functional e-commerce landing page for a jewellery brand that balances traditional luxury with Gen Z aesthetics. Use a soft, culturally rich color palette (warm gold, rose beige, muted teal) mixed with modern accents like gradients or glassmorphism. The layout should be clean but expressive. At the top, include a sticky navigation bar with a minimalist logo, search bar, category menu (like ‘Traditional’, ‘Contemporary’, ‘Wedding’), and icons for wishlist and cart. Feature a split hero section: on the left, a bold, editorial-style image of a traditional bridal jewellery set; on the right, a playful Gen Z-style vertical video or carousel showing mix-and-match styling tips. Add CTA buttons like 'Shop Now', 'Build Your Look', and 'Try Virtually'. Below, highlight product drops with clean card layouts, microinteractions, and trending tags like ‘Bestseller’, ‘Made in India’, or ‘Gold Under ₹10K’. Include sections for customer reviews, influencer picks, and a trust banner showing ‘Free Shipping’, ‘Secure Payments’, and ‘Easy Returns’. The typography should blend modern sans-serif (for CTAs/text) with subtle traditional flair in headers. Optimized for mobile-first viewing.

# openAI * Prompt 23
 * Page Link: https://sora.com/g/gen_01jr34c4c8ek0b0r58wagtd55w
 * Prompt:Aquí tienes un prompt optimizado y detallado para colocar en Sora, combinando la estructura anterior y el efecto visual de esta última imagen: --- **Prompt Sora para generar video:** *Crea una versión creativa, cinematográfica y visualmente rica, inspirada en el estilo de "The Comforting Illusion". En una escena ambientada en un elegante interior clásico con paredes decoradas, se encuentra un gran cuadro con una pintura realista de un río tranquilo rodeado por árboles frondosos y pequeños botes flotando pacíficamente. De repente, ocurre un efecto surrealista impactante: el agua de la pintura cobra vida y fluye dinámicamente fuera del lienzo, desbordándose hacia el suelo con fluidez y realismo cinematográfico, inundando lentamente la habitación. Usa iluminación suave y natural, tonos neutros y fríos, con detalles cinematográficos cuidados, generando una sensación de sorpresa pero manteniendo la estética sofisticada y envolvente del concepto original.* ---

The title "ROARING TWENTIES: 1920s" should be integrated stylishly, near the top in a bold Art Deco font. Overall Style & Mood: This must be a stunning masterpiece of hyper-realistic illustration, blending historical figures and scenes into a seamless, energetic montage. The style captures the essence of the Roaring Twenties – its glamour, its rapid change, its explosive culture, its hidden dangers, and its sheer energy – all rendered with vibrant, saturated colors and sharp, modern cinematic detail. The mood is exhilarating, fast-paced, glamorous, slightly dangerous, and full of life, reflecting the era's nickname. Crucially, the final image must be impeccably clean, sharp, high-resolution, with absolutely no film grain, scratches, stains, or artificial aging. Composition: A dynamic, layered montage composition is essential. Avoid a static grid. Use strong diagonal lines, perhaps suggested by Art Deco motifs integrated into the framing or transitions between vignettes. Elements should overlap and flow into each other, creating a sense of bustling activity and depth. Feature key figures prominently but integrated within the broader tapestry of the era. Key Elements (Include these specific items plus 1-2 additional contextual elements): Prominent Figures & Action: Louis Armstrong (Center Stage Energy): A hyper-realistic, dynamic depiction of a young, energetic Louis Armstrong passionately playing his trumpet. Capture the intensity in his expression, perhaps cheeks puffed, eyes focused or closed in concentration, sweat gleaming under vibrant stage lights. Position him centrally or slightly off-center, radiating musical energy. Clara Bow (The "It" Girl Glamour): A stunning, hyper-realistic portrait vignette of Clara Bow, embodying the flapper spirit. Use focused, flattering, almost sparkling lighting. Josephine Baker (Dynamic Performer): A dynamic, hyper-realistic portrait vignette of Josephine Baker captured mid-performance. Show her characteristic energy and captivating stage presence – perhaps in a stylish, feathered, or shimmering stage outfit striking a bold, confident pose. Emphasize movement and charisma under dramatic stage lighting. Charlie Chaplin (Iconic Comedy): A realistic depiction of Charlie Chaplin in his beloved "Tramp" persona (baggy pants, tight coat, bowler hat, mustache, cane). Capture him in a moment of dynamic physical comedy – perhaps precariously balancing, reacting with wide eyes, or executing a nimble maneuver with his cane. Babe Ruth (Sporting Legend): A dynamic, hyper-realistic action shot of Babe Ruth in his New York Yankees uniform, captured at the peak of his powerful baseball bat swing. Show the focused determination on his face, the blur of the bat, perhaps the baseball just connecting or flying off. Background hints at a cheering stadium crowd. Al Capone (Menacing Presence): A realistic, imposing depiction of Al Capone. Show him sharply dressed in a pinstripe suit and fedora, looking intimidatingly towards the viewer or overseeing a scene. Crucially, he holds a realistic Thompson submachine gun ("Tommy Gun") prominently but perhaps casually, signifying his dangerous power. Background could hint at a shadowy backroom or distillery. Technological & Cultural Elements: Harlem Renaissance Scene (Cultural Explosion): A vibrant vignette capturing the energy of the Harlem Renaissance. Show stylishly dressed African American musicians playing jazz instruments (saxophone, upright bass, piano partially visible) in a lively, crowded club setting. Include elegantly dressed patrons and perhaps a couple dancing energetically (Lindy Hop hints). Use dynamic, warm, colorful lighting. Ford Model A (Accessible Modernity): A gleaming, hyper-realistic depiction of a brand-new Ford Model A (accurate 1927-1931 design), perhaps in a bold color like deep blue or green. Show it parked proudly on a bustling city street with Art Deco buildings in the background, or driving dynamically. Emphasize its clean lines and shiny finish. Phonograph & Records (Home Entertainment): A realistic, detailed close-up or vignette of an ornate 1920s wind-up phonograph with a large, polished brass or wood horn. Show a spinning shellac record (78 rpm) on the turntable, perhaps with vibrant, period-style record labels visible on other records nearby. Early Radio Set (Mass Communication): A realistic depiction of a beautiful cathedral-style or sophisticated box radio from the 1920s, featuring polished wood and intricate details. Perhaps show glowing vacuum tubes subtly visible through vents or a warm light emanating from the dial. The Charleston Dance (Social Energy): Dynamic figures (a stylish flapper couple) captured mid-energetic Charleston dance step. Show the blur of movement in their fringed dresses and tailored suits, their joyful, exuberant expressions under bright party lights. Prohibition Element (Contrast/Conflict): A visually striking element representing Prohibition – perhaps federal agents dramatically raiding a speakeasy, smashing bottles/barrels OR a glamorous, secretive speakeasy bar scene with patrons discreetly enjoying cocktails, bartenders mixing drinks behind a hidden bar. Choose one strong visual. Art Deco Influence: Overall Integration: Weave Art Deco stylistic motifs throughout the composition – use sharp geometric patterns, sunbursts, zigzags, or streamlined curves in background architectural details (skyscraper spires, theater marquees), in the transitions between vignettes, or potentially as a subtle framing element for the entire poster. The title font must strongly reflect the Art Deco style (e.g., Broadway, Peignot-like, stylized geometric). Lighting, Color & Overall Finish: Lighting: Bright, dynamic, high-contrast, and cinematic. Utilize dramatic spotlights (stage performers, Capone), glamorous soft lighting (Clara Bow), bright daylight (Babe Ruth, Model A), warm, inviting interior light (Harlem Renaissance, speakeasy, phonograph/radio), and energetic flashing lights (Charleston). Color Palette: BOLD, VIBRANT, and SATURATED. This is paramount for the Roaring Twenties feel. Use the rich golds, silvers, blacks, deep reds, emerald greens, and electric blues characteristic of Art Deco and 1920s luxury. Feature bright colors in clothing, cars, stage lighting, and signage. High contrast is essential. Overall Finish: Hyperrealistic detail in every aspect: textures of fabric (silk, sequins, beads, wool suits), metallic sheen (instruments, Tommy Gun, car chrome, phonograph horn), polished wood grain, shellac records, skin tones, hair textures, architectural details. CRITICAL: Absolutely no film grain, dust, scratches, blurriness, or artificial aging. The image must be pristine, sharp, clean, high-resolution, and possess a polished, modern finish while depicting the historical era.

A small white teardrop-shaped patch glows beneath its right eye, and a darker spot marks its left hind leg. Its large deep brown eyes squint slightly in concentration beneath a welding visor that’s clearly too big — the sides droop past its cheeks like a helmet borrowed from someone five times its size. The ears poke out awkwardly, bent at the tips. It wears a faded ash-gray short-sleeve t-shirt with small holes near the shoulders, the collar stretched and slipping off one shoulder. The shirt bunches near its tiny elbows. Its oversized charcoal-gray sweatpants pool at its ankles and drag slightly over the can’s rim, frayed and stained with dust and concrete. With both tiny paws gripping a full-size welding torch — clearly too heavy — the dog leans forward toward a sheet of metal propped against stacked bricks. Sparks shoot out in bright white and electric blue arcs. One paw grips tighter while the other wobbles slightly under the weight, but the weld holds steady. It looks up through the tinted visor with quiet intensity, no smile, just focus. Background: A worker nearby, frozen mid-bite with a lunchbox in hand, stares in disbelief. Another worker crouches to record the moment, grinning. A bucket of bent metal rods and unused gear surrounds the makeshift welding station — making the dog appear even smaller. The entire scene captures raw contrast: oversized equipment, oversized gear, oversized job — handled by one unbelievably tiny, determined dog.

The stronger the moat, the longer a company can stay profitable.” Castle chibi waves from behind wide water filled with: 💡 Brand Power (e.g., Coca-Cola) 🧱 High Switching Costs (e.g., enterprise software) 🛒 Cost Advantage (e.g., Walmart) 🧬 Network Effects (e.g., Amazon, Google) ⚙️ Efficient Scale (e.g., railways, utilities) ✅ 🕵️‍♂️ "How Buffett Spots a Moat" – Chibi Buffett has a checklist: ✅ Consistent Profitability ✅ High ROE/ROCE ✅ Predictable Business ✅ Loyal Customers ✅ Ability to Reinvest Profits Thought bubble: “I don’t just buy stocks—I buy businesses I’d hold forever.” ✅ 📉 "What Happens Without a Moat?" – A sad little company chibi with no moat gets attacked by mini competitors: Price wars 💥 New entrants 🏃‍♂️ Shrinking margins 📉 Caption: “No moat = no pricing power = no long-term edge.” ✅ 📈 "Why Moats Matter for Investors" – Calm investor chibi smiles as their portfolio tree labeled “Moat Stocks 🌳” grows over time.
